[cybersecurity_incidents_raw_12000.csv](https://github.com/user-attachments/files/25202386/cybersecurity_incidents_raw_12000.csv)# Cyber Security Analysis Dashboard

## üìå Project Overview
This project focuses on analyzing cybersecurity incidents across different departments and risk levels using Power BI.

## üõ† Tools Used
- Power BI
- DAX
- Power Query

## üìä Key Features
- KPI cards for total incidents and resolution performance
- Risk-level categorization (Low, Medium, High, Critical)
- Interactive slicers for department and date-based analysis

## üìà Insights
- High-risk incidents were concentrated in specific departments
- Incident trends showed periodic spikes requiring proactive monitoring
